  <script type="text/javascript">
   var width = null;
var orientation = null;
var headerFixedClass = false;
var inPageVatStatus = false;
var vatSwitchInProgress = false;

var urlMappings = {
				'us': 'siteground.com',				'uk': 'siteground.co.uk',				'es': 'siteground.es',				'it': 'it.siteground.com',				'de': 'siteground.com',				'eu': 'siteground.com',				'au': 'siteground.com',				'la': 'es.siteground.com',				'ww': 'siteground.com'			};

var hostnamePrefix = null;

var sCoRegionMapping = {
		'us': 'MWc9PQ==',		'uk': 'MEE9PQ==',		'es': 'MFE9PQ==',		'it': 'MUE9PQ==',		'de': 'MDBVPQ==',		'eu': 'MXc9PQ==',		'au': 'Mnc9PQ==',		'la': 'Mmc9PQ==',		'ww': 'MHc9PQ=='	};
	var hostPrefix = 'www.';

function formatPriceHalfDown(value) {
	var exp = -2;
	value = +value;
	exp = +exp;
	type = 'round';

    	var difference = (parseFloat(value) * 100) - (Math.floor(value * 100));
	if (difference <= 0.5 && difference !== 0) {
		type = 'floor';
	}
    
	// If the value is not a number or the exp is not an integer...
	if (isNaN(value)) {
		return 0;
	}

	// Shift
	value = value.toString().split('e');
	value = Math[type](+(value[0] + 'e' + (value[1] ? (+value[1] - exp) : -exp)));
	// Shift back
	value = value.toString().split('e');
	value = +(value[0] + 'e' + (value[1] ? (+value[1] + exp) : exp));

	return value.toFixed(2);
}

function fixLongFloatNumbers(number) {
	return parseFloat(number.toFixed(4));
}

function vatMultiply(string, multi)
{
	var amountWithVat = 0;
	var returnStr = '';

	// In case there are empty vatPriceElement spans
	if (string === '') return '';

	var thousandsRegex = /\B(?=(\d{3})+(?!\d))/g;
	var currency = string.charAt(0);
	var amount = string.substr(1);

	// Calculate
	amountWithVat = fixLongFloatNumbers(parseFloat(amount.replace(',','')) * multi);
	returnStr = formatPriceHalfDown(amountWithVat);
	// Add curreny add commas for thousands
	returnStr = currency + String(returnStr).replace(thousandsRegex, ",");
	return returnStr;
}

function toggleVatIncluded()
{
    if (vatSwitchInProgress)
		return;

	vatSwitchInProgress = true;

	var enabled = !inPageVatStatus;

	document.cookie = "includingVat=" + (enabled ? 1 : 0) + ";expires=0";

	var vatPercent = 21;

	var taxName = 'VAT';
	
	var multi = enabled ? ((vatPercent+100)/100) : 1/((vatPercent+100)/100);
	$('.vatPriceElement').each(function()
	{
		if ($(this).prop('id') == 'promoBannerMonthlyPrice' || $(this).prop('id') == 'promoSpecialPrice')
			$(this).html(vatMultiply($(this).html(),multi));
		else
			$(this).text(vatMultiply($(this).text(),multi));
	});

	if (enabled)
	{
		$('.vatNoticeText').each(function()
		{
			$(this).text( $(this).text().
                replace('Excluding '+taxName,'Including '+taxName).
                replace('Excl. '+taxName, 'Incl. '+taxName).
                replace('Prices exclude '+taxName, 'Prices include '+taxName).
                replace('exclude VAT', 'include VAT').
                replace('Prices in AUD exclude '+taxName, 'Prices in AUD include '+taxName).
                replace('exclude '+taxName, 'include '+taxName)
            );
		});

		$('.vatNoticeText').each(function()
		{
		    $(this).text( $(this).text().replace('AUD Excluding 10% GST','AUD Including 10% GST').replace('AUD Excl. 10% GST', 'AUD Incl. 10% GST') );
		});

				    $('#vatSwitcher').find('.js-vat-price-info').text('Prices include ' + taxName);
		    $('#vatSwitcher a strong').text('Show prices without ' + taxName);
			}
	else
	{
		$('.vatNoticeText').each(function()
		{
			$(this).text( $(this).text().
                replace('Including '+taxName,'Excluding '+taxName).
                replace('Incl. '+taxName, 'Excl. '+taxName).
                replace('Prices include '+taxName, 'Prices exclude '+taxName).
                replace('include VAT', 'exclude VAT').
                replace('Prices in AUD include '+taxName, 'Prices in AUD exclude '+taxName).
                replace('include '+taxName, 'exclude '+taxName)
            );
		});

		$('.vatNoticeText').each(function()
		        {
		            $(this).text( $(this).text().replace('AUD Including 10% GST','AUD Excluding 10% GST').replace('AUD Incl. 10% GST', 'AUD Excl. 10% GST') );
		        });

					$('#vatSwitcher').find('.js-vat-price-info').text('Prices exclude ' + taxName);
			$('#vatSwitcher a strong').text('Show prices with ' + taxName);
			}

	inPageVatStatus = !inPageVatStatus;
	vatSwitchInProgress = false;
	return;
}

function fixedHeader()
{
	if (width <= 1023 && (orientation == 0 || orientation == 180))
	{
		if (($(document).scrollTop() >= 1))
		{
			if (headerFixedClass == false)
			{
				$('#header').addClass('fixed');
				headerFixedClass = true;
			}
		}
		else
		{
			if (headerFixedClass == true)
			{
				$('#header').removeClass('fixed');
				headerFixedClass = false;
			}
		}
	}

	if ((orientation == -90 || orientation == 90) && headerFixedClass == true)
	{
		$('#header').removeClass('fixed');
		headerFixedClass = false;
	}
}

$(window).on('touchmove scroll', function() {
	fixedHeader();
});

$(document).ready( function() {
	var verticalMenu = null;
	width = window.innerWidth;
	orientation = window.orientation;

	fixedHeader();

	if (width <= 1023 && !verticalMenu) {
		verticalMenu = true;
		$('#main-navigation').insertAfter('#container');
	}

	else if (width >= 1024 && (orientation == -90 || orientation == 90)) {
		$('.open-main-nav').css('display', 'none');
	}

	$('.open-main-nav').on('click', function(e) {
		if(!$(this).hasClass('active')) {
			$('#container, #header, #main-navigation, #footer').addClass('slide-left');
			$(this).addClass('active');
		}
		else {
			$('#container, #header, #main-navigation, #footer').removeClass('slide-left');
			$(this).removeClass('active');
		}
		e.preventDefault();
		e.stopPropagation();
	});

    //fix for mobile hover
    $('#main-navigation').doubleTapToGo();

    $(window).on('orientationchange', function() {
		width = window.innerWidth;
		orientation = window.orientation;
		fixedHeader();
		if ( width >= 1024 && (orientation == -90 || orientation == 90) ) {
			$('.open-main-nav').css('display', 'none');
			$('#main-navigation').insertAfter('#header');
		}
		else {
			$('.open-main-nav').css('display', 'block');
		}
	});

	$(window).on('resize', function() {
		width = window.innerWidth;
		fixedHeader();
		if ( width <= 1023 && !verticalMenu ) {
			verticalMenu = true;
			$('#main-navigation').insertAfter('#container');
		}
		else if (width >= 1023 && verticalMenu) {
			verticalMenu = false;
			$('#container, #main-navigation, #footer').removeClass('slide-left');
			$('.open-main-nav').removeClass('active');
			$('#main-navigation').insertAfter('.header-logo');
		}
	});

	$('#main-navigation').on('click', function(e) {
		e.stopPropagation();
	});

	$(document).on('click', function(e) {
		if ($('.open-main-nav').hasClass('active')) {
			$('#container, #header, #main-navigation, #footer').removeClass('slide-left');
			$('.open-main-nav').removeClass('active');
		}
	});

	//Region Drop Down In Footer

	$('#choosen').on('click', function(e) {
		if ($('#choosen').hasClass('active')) {
			$('#choosen, .companylocation').removeClass('active');
		}
		else {
			$('.companylocation, #choosen').addClass('active');
		}
		e.preventDefault();
		e.stopPropagation();
	});


	$(document).on('click', function(e) {
		if ($('.companylocation').hasClass('active')) {
			$('.companylocation').removeClass('active');
		}

	});

});

$(function(){
	$('#footerSearchForm').on( 'submit', function( el ) {
		// some bot blocking
		if ( $('#footerSearchInput').val().match( /WCRTEST/ ))
			el.preventDefault();
	});

	$('#footerSearchFormHeader').on( 'submit', function( el ) {
		// some bot blocking
		if ( $('#footerSearchInputHeader').val().match( /WCRTEST/ ))
			el.preventDefault();
	});

	$('#footerSearchButton').on( 'click', function( el ) {
		el.preventDefault();
		if ( !$('#footerSearchInput').val().match( /^\s*$/ ) )
			$('#footerSearchForm').submit();

		return false;
	});

	var params = [];

	// bind click on the locations drop-down
	$(".companylocation ul.locations li a").click( function( event ) {
		event.preventDefault();
		var elemClass = $(this).children('span').attr('class');
		// the country location is inside the class of the a > span
		var countryMatchRegex = new RegExp("\\b[a-z][a-z]\\b");
		var locale = countryMatchRegex.exec( elemClass );

		if( urlMappings.hasOwnProperty( locale ) ) {
            var prefix = 'www.';
            if (hostnamePrefix) {
                prefix=hostnamePrefix;
            }
            if (prefix == 'www.' && !urlMappings[ locale ].match(/^siteground/)) {
                prefix = '';
            }
            url = window.location.protocol + "//" + prefix + urlMappings[ locale ];
			if (urlMappings[ locale ] == 'siteground.com')
			{
				params.push( {
					value: sCoRegionMapping[ locale ],
					label: 'reg'
				});
			}

			submitRedirect(url, params);
		}
	});
});


function additem(form, name, value)
{
	item = document.createElement("input");
	item.setAttribute('type', 'hidden');
	item.setAttribute('name', name);
	item.setAttribute('value', value);
	form.appendChild(item);
}


function submitRedirect(url, params, newTab)
{
	 var form = document.createElement("form");
	 var hiddenFieldURL = document.createElement("input");

	 form.setAttribute("method", 'POST');
	 form.setAttribute("action", '/redirect');

	 if (newTab) {
	 	form.setAttribute('target', '_blank');
	 }

     hiddenFieldURL.setAttribute("type", "hidden");
     hiddenFieldURL.setAttribute("name", 'redirectURL');
     hiddenFieldURL.setAttribute("value", url);

     form.appendChild(hiddenFieldURL);

	 document.body.appendChild(form,url);

	 // Params
	 for(i in params)
		 additem(form, 'params['+params[i].label+']', params[i].value);

	 form.submit();
}

function OpenTermsWindow(theURL,winName,features) {
	window.open(theURL,'terms','scrollbars=yes,width=600,height=500');
}
